# FCN

## Dataset

```{.python .input  n=1}
from mxnet import image

voc_root = '../data/VOCdevkit/VOC2012'

def read_images(root=voc_root, train=True):
    txt_fname = root+'/ImageSets/Segmentation/'+(
        'train.txt' if train else 'val.txt')
    with open(txt_fname, 'r') as f:
        images = f.read().split() 
    n = len(images)
    data, label = [None]*n, [None]*n
    for i, fname in enumerate(images):
        data[i] = image.imread('%s/JPEGImages/%s.jpg'%(            
            root, fname))
        label[i] = image.imread('%s/SegmentationClass/%s.png'%(
            root, fname))  
    return data, label
        
train_images, train_labels = read_images()



```

```{.python .input  n=2}
import sys
sys.path.append('..')
import utils

imgs = []
for i in range(3):
    imgs += [train_images[i], train_labels[i]]
        
utils.show_images(imgs, nrows=3, ncols=2, figsize=(8,12))
[im.shape for im in imgs]
```

```{.python .input  n=3}
def rand_crop(data, label, height, width):
    data, rect = image.random_crop(data, (width, height))
    label = image.fixed_crop(label, *rect)
    return data, label

imgs = []
for _ in range(3):
    imgs += rand_crop(train_images[0], train_labels[0], 
                      200, 300)
    
utils.show_images(imgs, nrows=3, ncols=2, figsize=(8,12))
```

```{.python .input  n=4}
classes = ['background','aeroplane','bicycle','bird','boat',
           'bottle','bus','car','cat','chair','cow','diningtable',
           'dog','horse','motorbike','person','potted plant',
           'sheep','sofa','train','tv/monitor']
# RGB color for each class
colormap = [[0,0,0],[128,0,0],[0,128,0], [128,128,0], [0,0,128], 
            [128,0,128],[0,128,128],[128,128,128],[64,0,0],[192,0,0],
            [64,128,0],[192,128,0],[64,0,128],[192,0,128],
            [64,128,128],[192,128,128],[0,64,0],[128,64,0],
            [0,192,0],[128,192,0],[0,64,128]]

len(classes), len(colormap)
```

```{.python .input  n=5}
import numpy as np
from mxnet import nd

cm2lbl = - np.ones(256**3)
for i,cm in enumerate(colormap):    
    cm2lbl[(cm[0]*256+cm[1])*256+cm[2]] = i
    
def image2label(im):
    data = im.astype('int32').asnumpy()
    idx = (data[:,:,0]*256+data[:,:,1])*256+data[:,:,2]
    return nd.array(cm2lbl[idx])
```

```{.python .input  n=6}
y = image2label(train_labels[0])
```

```{.python .input  n=7}
from mxnet import gluon
from mxnet import nd

rgb_mean = nd.array([123, 117, 104])

class VOCSegDataset(gluon.data.Dataset):
    
    def _filter(self, images):
        return [im for im in images if (
            im.shape[0] >= self.crop_size[0] and
            im.shape[1] >= self.crop_size[1])]  
            
    def __init__(self, train, crop_size):
        self.crop_size = crop_size
        data, label = read_images(train=train)
        self.data = self._filter(data)
        self.label = self._filter(label)
        print('Read '+str(len(self.data))+' examples')
        
    def __getitem__(self, idx):
        data, label = rand_crop(
            self.data[idx], self.label[idx],
            *self.crop_size)
        #data, label = self.data[idx], self.label[idx]
        #data = image.imresize(data, 400, 300)
        data = data.transpose((2,0,1)).astype('float32')# - rgb_mean.reshape((3,1,1))
        label = image2label(label)
        #z = np.histogram(label.asnumpy(), bins=np.arange(-1,20))[0]
        #label = (np.argmax(z[2:])+1).astype('float32')
        return data, label
        
    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.data)
```

```{.python .input  n=8}
input_shape = (320, 480) # height width
voc_train = VOCSegDataset(True, input_shape)
voc_test = VOCSegDataset(False, input_shape)
```

```{.python .input  n=13}
def get_upsampling_weight(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size):
    """Make a 2D bilinear kernel suitable for upsampling"""
    factor = (kernel_size + 1) // 2
    if kernel_size % 2 == 1:
        center = factor - 1
    else:
        center = factor - 0.5
    og = np.ogrid[:kernel_size, :kernel_size]
    filt = (1 - abs(og[0] - center) / factor) * \
           (1 - abs(og[1] - center) / factor)
    weight = np.zeros((in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, kernel_size),
                      dtype=np.float64)
    weight[range(in_channels), range(out_channels), :, :] = filt
    return nd.array(weight).astype('float32')

```

```{.python .input}
from mxnet.gluon.model_zoo import vision as models
pretrained_net = models.resnet18_v2(pretrained=True)

from mxnet import gluon, nd
import sys
sys.path.append('..')
import utils

from mxnet.gluon import nn
from mxnet import init

#batch_size = 16
#input_shape = (320, 480) # height width


num_classes=21

output = nn.HybridSequential()
with output.name_scope():    
    output.add(
        nn.Conv2D(num_classes, kernel_size=1),
        nn.Conv2DTranspose(num_classes, kernel_size=64, padding=16,strides=32)
    )    

net = nn.HybridSequential()
for layer in pretrained_net.features[:-2]:
    net.add(layer)
net.add(output)

output.initialize(init=init.Xavier())
#net.collect_params().initialize(init=init.Xavier(),force_reinit=True)

ctx = utils.try_all_gpus()

net.collect_params().reset_ctx(ctx)
#output.collect_params().reset_ctx(ctx)


#net.initialize(ctx=ctx, init=init.Xavier())
loss = gluon.loss.SoftmaxCrossEntropyLoss(axis=1)  

print(input_shape)
print(net(nd.zeros((batch_size, 3, *input_shape), ctx=ctx[0])).shape)

trainer = gluon.Trainer(net.collect_params(),
                        'sgd', {'learning_rate': .1, 'wd':0.0001})

weight = output[-1].params.get('weight')
shape = weight.data(ctx[0]).shape
zz = get_upsampling_weight(*shape[0:3])
weight.set_data(zz)
#print(net[-1][-1].params.get('weight').data(ctx[0]))

utils.train(train_data, test_data, net, loss,
            trainer, ctx, num_epochs=200)
```

from mxnet import gluon
from mxnet import init
from mxnet.gluon import nn
from utils import Residual

from mxnet.gluon.model_zoo import vision as model
pretrained_net = models.resnet18_v2(pretrained=True)

num_classes = len(classes)
net = nn.HybridSequential()
with net.name_scope():
    for i in range(
    net.add(
        nn.BatchNorm(),
        nn.Conv2D(64, kernel_size=3, strides=1),
        nn.MaxPool2D(pool_size=3, strides=2), # 1 / 2
        Residual(64),
        Residual(64),
        Residual(128, same_shape=False), # 1 / 4
        Residual(128),
        Residual(256, same_shape=False), # 1 / 8
        Residual(256),
        #nn.GlobalAvgPool2D(),
        nn.Conv2D(num_classes, kernel_size=1),
        nn.Conv2DTranspose(num_classes, kernel_size=8, padding=0,strides=8)
    )
    
#ctx = utils.try_all_gpus()

#net.initialize(ctx=ctx, init=init.Xavier())
loss = gluon.loss.SoftmaxCrossEntropyLoss(axis=1)  

trainer = gluon.Trainer(net.collect_params(),
                        'sgd', {'learning_rate': 1})
utils.train(train_data, test_data, net, loss,
            trainer, ctx, num_epochs=100)
#yhat = net(data.as_in_context(ctx))
#l = loss(yhat, label)


# net.initialize()
#x = nd.random.uniform(shape=(1,3,256,256))
#net(x).shape

```{.python .input  n=27}
def predict(im):
    data = im.as_in_context(ctx[0])
    data = data.expand_dims(axis=0)
    print(data.shape)
    #data = im.astype('float32').as_in_context(ctx[0])
    #data = data.transpose((2,0,1)).expand_dims(axis=0)
    yhat = net(data)
    pred = nd.argmax(yhat, axis=1)
    return pred.reshape((pred.shape[1], pred.shape[2]))

i = 3
y = predict(voc_test[i][0])
y.shape

cm = np.array(colormap).astype('uint8')
z = y.astype('int32').asnumpy()

from matplotlib import pyplot as plt
plt.imshow(voc_test.data[i].asnumpy())
plt.show()

plt.show()

plt.show()
```
